wilzin belongs to a group of medicines called metabolism products . it is used in adults to treat a rare inherited defect in copper excretion in the liver , the eyes and the brain . this can lead to liver damage , neurological disorders , and damage of the intestine , which can cause its further accumulation in the body . if you are not sure , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before you are given this treatment .

filgrastim ratiopharm is a medicine that contains the active substance filgra stim , which belongs to a group of proteins called escherichia coli , a natural protein , called granulocytes , that is produced by the bone marrow to produce new blood cells . more blood cells are produced , and more white cells are formed . white cells help your body fight infection . filgrartim reduces the number of white blood cells that your body produces , but not all of them are produced by your body , especially when you are treated with the use of filgraltim ratioopharm , because it helps your body to fight infection more effectively than other medicines , such as chemotherapy , bone mmarrow transplantation , or severe chronic neutropenia ( dna ) in adults .

proquad is a vaccine against measles , mumps , rubella , and chickenpox ( varicella ) viruses . the vaccine contains antibodies to protect against the diseases that are caused by them . if you are not sure , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before you are given the vaccine . your doctor will test your child ' s immune system to see if the vaccine is working properly . you will also be given the antibodies to prevent diseases caused by these viruses , so it is important that you know how to prevent them from working . it is also important that your child does not have to be vaccinated . this means that the vaccine will be given to you at least 12 months after the vaccination is given . however , it is not known whether the vaccine may be effective for 9 months after national vaccination .

proquad is injected into a muscle , usually under the skin , in the thigh or arm area . injections are given to the muscle in the upper limb , and in the lower arm area at the injection site . if you have a blood clotting disorder or low levels of platelets , the vaccine will be given to you by your doctor or nurse . the vaccine is applied to the skin to reduce the risk of bleeding from the muscle . it is then injected directly into the blood vessel . you will not be able to see the difference between the dose and the time of injection . your doctor will tell you exactly how long you will receive .

incruse ellipta contains the active substance umeclidinium bromide . it belongs to a group of medicines called bronchodilators . this medicine is used to treat chronic obstructive pulmonary disease ( copd ) in adults . copd is a long - term condition that affects the lungs , causing breathing difficulties , difficulties in breathing , and tightening of the muscles in your body . when you take this medicine , you will feel tighter and tighter in your muscles , so that your breathing difficulties will be reduced . if you have copd and you have a sudden attack of breathlessness or wheezing , your doctor will tell you how to use it .

nucala contains mepolizumab , a monoclonal antibody , which is a type of protein . it is used to treat severe asthma in adults and adolescents aged 6 years and older . severe asthma is caused by the presence of many eosinophils , or white blood cells , in the lungs . this type of asthma is known as e . coli . asthmanucala is used for the treatment of asthma attacks caused by medicines called high dose inhalers . your asthma is treated with these medicines . these medicines are medicines called oral corticosteroids . the active substance in nucalal helps to treat your asthma . mepolizumab works by reducing the amount of interleukin -5 , an important protein in the body .

always use nucala exactly as your doctor has told you . check with your doctor , pharmacist or nurse if you are not sure . the recommended dose is one injection under the skin ( subcutaneous injection ) every 12 hours . each 100 mg injection is 1 ml of the pre - filled pen . your doctor will decide how much to inject . do not inject more than you should if your doctor tells you to . if the dose is too low , your doctor may decide to increase the dose . you will be given a different dose , depending on the type of treatment you will receive . this will help to control your asthma symptoms , such as attacks , and reduce the number of injections . it is important that you do not stop the treatment . however , you should continue to receive this medicine at the same time each day .
